***vertellen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vertellen.html>vertellen</a> (248)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vertellen.html>vertellen</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tellen.html>tellen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vertellen.html>vertellen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tell
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:verteld.html>verteld</a></b>. / <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vertelde.html>vertelde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I have <b><a href = vnd.unilang:told.html>told</a></b> him. / I <b><a href = vnd.unilang:told.html>told</a></b> him.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p>[A] <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vertellen.html>vertellen</a></b>
</p>

<ol><li>delay</li>

***vervelen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vervelen.html>vervelen</a> (5989)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vervelen.html>vervelen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to become or seem to be too much</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vervelen.html>vervelen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to annoy, to pester</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bore; inspire boredom in somebody</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be bored</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***vervelend.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vervelend.html>vervelend</a> (1914)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vervelend.html>vervelend</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vervelend.html>vervelender</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">vervelendst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>boring, uninteresting</li>

***vervliegen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vervliegen.html>vervliegen</a> (50382)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vervliegen.html>vervliegen</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vliegen.html>vliegen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vervliegen.html>vervliegen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to evaporate, to dissipate, to volatilise</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to evaporate, to disappear</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> e.g. of time</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fly away, to go away</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to flee, to escape</li></ol>

***vervoegen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vervoegen.html>vervoegen</a> (24695)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voegen.html>voegen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vervoegen.html>vervoegen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to conjugate</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">proscribed</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to join</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Some <a href = vnd.unilang:speakers.html>speakers</a> use this verb to mean "to join". Many <a href = vnd.unilang:speakers.html>speakers</a> and language organisations consider this usage nonstandard and advise <a href = vnd.unilang:speakers.html>speakers</a> to use, among other <a href = vnd.unilang:things.html>things</a>, "<a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:ver.html>ver</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:voegen.html>voegen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a>" or "<a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aansluiten.html>aansluiten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a>" instead.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
